<Rate>5< /Rate>< Text>
Probably the best tea in the area. As a lay person, it feels like each of their teas is more dynamic than the offerings at the typical boba shop. The defining feature here is the ability of the person handling the orders to describe and explain all the different flavors on offer. That level of service makes it feel like a premium experience. Echos of Portland in the food culture here. The boba is fresh to the point of being warm. Not overly sweet though. It's a bit more pricey than the typical boba shop but it feels like you're getting that proportionate premium experience.

Biggest downsides would be the reliable line. They work through it pretty quickly but there is a wait. It's also important to dial in your sweetness. Fortunately they're generous about reworking the drink i you don't like it. Rising pheonix is great. The Honey Gyuro is my current jam. Red jade is a bit more subtle than Omomo's offering and I prefer this version.< /Text>

<Time>1567592248565< /Time>< Review>
Old classic Korean-Chinese restaurant that's been open for over 20 years. The entrees there are excellent, and I'd say this is the some of the best jjajangmyeon you can get in the area. In fact, the jjajangmyeon, a staple of Korean-Chinese cuisine, is better than that of quite established Koreatown places such as The Dragon. In other words, that's kind of a big deal. That just hints at how well done the food is here.

The main competitor that I know of in the IE with similar cuisine is China Point, and Fu Lin blows it out of the water in both entrees and noodles.<//Review>

<resp>{'time': 1630346511070, 'text': 'Thank you so much Cheryl! It was a pleasure workin with you!'}< /resp>< Text>
On June 16 our church sanctuary wing in  Yucca Valley completely flooded (pastor‚Äôs study, 2 anterooms, sanctuary -112 person capacity- foyer, mother‚Äôs room and 2 bathrooms).  In areas of the sanctuary itself there was an inch plus of standing water.
I called a businessman friend in Redlands and he recommended Padgett‚Äôs Fire and Flood Restoration.  I called and talked to Wyatt Padgett who came up immediately to assess and evaluate, talked to our insurance to get things moving, and had a company to do hazmat testing on site that day so that we could be ready to remove drywall and insulation. He also had a crew there early on to do emergency water extraction and set up 40 + heater fans for about a week to dry out carpet, pews, etc. They had to remove 2 feet of drywall and insulation throughout the whole wing, there were areas that were challenging because this facility is 54 years old.
We found Padgett‚Äôs to be an awesome company to work with. The shredded beef tacos were the best  we've ever had and definitely worth going back for! Rice and beans are two of the things that you measure a Mexican restaurant by and we both thought that they're were good. The platter that the food is served on makes for an absolutely beautiful presentation!
The salsa and chips were a bit disappointing. The salsa was very heavy on the oregano and tasted like the tomatoes came from a can. The chips were crispy but had an aftertaste that was rather unpleasant. The red sauce on the enchiladas was very mild and lacked in flavor but the cheese was plentiful.
We're definitely planning on going back when we're in the area again because.. those shredded beef tacos were amazing!
The servers never lacked in smiles and were quick to notice if drinks needed to be refreshed.</review>
